## count lines of code for each project
for d in ./*/ ; do (cd "$d" && echo ; echo "$d" && cloc --vcs git) >> output.txt; done; cat output.txt | grep -v "Sav\|sav\|compl\|Uniq\|Count" > lines_of_code.txt
